>>>>>>>>>>PROMPT_START: 3119
Translate the following Python code into an equivalent C++ implementation.

```
import math

def is_prime(number):
    if number <= 1:
        return False
    for i in range(2, int(math.sqrt(number)) + 1):
        if number % i == 0:
            return False
    return True
```

>>>>>>>>>>PROMPT_START: 3615
Rewrite the following Python code to be more efficient: 
```python
def least_common_multiple(a, b):
    if a > b:
        smaller = b
    else:
        smaller = a
    for i in range(1, smaller+1):
        if ((a % i == 0) and (b % i == 0)):
            gcd = i
    return (a * b) // gcd
```
